</aside>
<b>GOT7</b> (갓세븐) is a seven-member boy group under <a href="/wiki/Kakao_Entertainment" title="Kakao Entertainment">Kakao Entertainment</a>. Formed by <a href="/wiki/JYP_Entertainment" title="JYP Entertainment">JYP Entertainment</a>, they debuted on January 16, 2014 with their first mini album <i><a href="/wiki/Got_It%3F" title="Got It?">Got It?</a></i>.
</p><p>They are multinational with members from South Korea, Hong Kong, Thailand and the United States.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="History">History</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-action="edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fkpop.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGOT7%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D1&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pre-debut">Pre-debut</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-action="edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fkpop.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGOT7%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D2&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Prior to their debut in GOT7, members JB and Jinyoung (formerly Junior) had debuted as a duo, named <a href="/wiki/JJ_Project" title="JJ Project">JJ Project</a>. Members Jackson, Mark, Bambam and Yugyeom also briefly appeared in the reality survival program <i>WIN: Who Is Next</i>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-2"><a href="#cite_note-2"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>1<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="2014:_Debut_with_.22Girls_Girls_Girls.22.2C_Got_It.3F.2C_Got_Love.2C_Japanese_debut_with_.22Around_The_World.22.2C_Identify"></span><span class="mw-headline" id='2014:_Debut_with_"Girls_Girls_Girls",_Got_It?,_Got_Love,_Japanese_debut_with_"Around_The_World",_Identify'>2014: Debut with "Girls Girls Girls", <i>Got It?</i>, <i>Got Love</i>, Japanese debut with "Around The World", <i>Identify</i></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-action="edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fkpop.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGOT7%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D3&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb mw-halign-left show-info-icon" style="width: 220px" typeof="mw:File/Thumb"> <a class="mw-file-description image" href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/kpop/images/0/02/GOT7_Got_It_group_concept_photo_1.png/revision/latest?cb=20250306145419"><img alt="GOT7 Got It group concept photo 1" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-key="GOT7_Got_It_group_concept_photo_1.png" data-image-name="GOT7 Got It group concept photo 1.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/kpop/images/0/02/GOT7_Got_It_group_concept_photo_1.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20250306145419" decoding="async" height="147" loading="lazy" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="220"/></a> <noscript><a class="mw-file-description image" href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/kpop/images/0/02/GOT7_Got_It_group_concept_photo_1.png/revision/latest?cb=20250306145419"><img alt="GOT7 Got It group concept photo 1" class="thumbimage" data-image-key="GOT7_Got_It_group_concept_photo_1.png" data-image-name="GOT7 Got It group concept photo 1.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/kpop/images/0/02/GOT7_Got_It_group_concept_photo_1.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20250306145419" decoding="async" height="147" loading="lazy" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/kpop/images/0/02/GOT7_Got_It_group_concept_photo_1.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20250306145419" width="220"/></a></noscript> <figcaption class="thumbcaption"> <a class="info-icon" href="/wiki/File:GOT7_Got_It_group_concept_photo_1.png"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> <p class="caption">Concept photo for <i><a href="/wiki/Got_It%3F" title="Got It?">Got It?</a></i></p> </figcaption> </figure>
<p>From the beginning, GOT7 was a group that JYP Entertainment aimed to promote internationally, with members from Hong Kong, Thailand and the United States.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-koreaherald.com_3-0"><a href="#cite_note-koreaherald.com-3"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>2<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> They officially debuted in January 2014 with lead single "Girls Girls Girls". The track’s music video amassed more than a million views in two days, and its choreography featured acrobatic, martial arts-inspired moves.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-4"><a href="#cite_note-4"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>3<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> The song’s mini album, <i><a href="/wiki/Got_It%3F" title="Got It?">Got It?</a></i>, was released a few days later.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-koreaherald.com_3-1"><a href="#cite_note-koreaherald.com-3"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>2<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> It hit number 1 of the Billboard World Albums Chart.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-5"><a href="#cite_note-5"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>4<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p><p>In April, GOT7 had two debut showcases in Japan.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-6"><a href="#cite_note-6"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>5<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> JYP Entertainment announced in May 2014 that GOT7 would have their first comeback in June.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-7"><a href="#cite_note-7"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>6<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> Individual member teasers were released one after the other before the mini-album <i><a href="/wiki/Got_Love" title="Got Love">Got Love</a></i> was released on June 23 with the music video of its title track, "A".<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-8"><a href="#cite_note-8"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>7<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p><p>GOT7 kicked off their first Japan Tour in October, a few weeks before they made their Japanese debut on October 22 with the single "<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Around_the_World" title="Around the World">Around the World</a>".<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-9"><a href="#cite_note-9"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>8<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> Less than a month later, GOT7 came back with their first full-length album, <i><a href="/wiki/Identify" title="Identify">Identify</a></i>, which was released on November 18.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-10"><a href="#cite_note-10"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>9<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> "Stop Stop It", the title track, was described as a hip-hop song with heavy bass and an addictive beat.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-11"><a href="#cite_note-11"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>10<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="2015:_.22Love_Train.22.2C_Just_Right.2C_.22Laugh_Laugh_Laugh.22.2C_Mad.2C_Mad_Winter_Edition"></span><span class="mw-headline" id='2015:_"Love_Train",_Just_Right,_"Laugh_Laugh_Laugh",_Mad,_Mad_Winter_Edition'>2015: "Love Train", <i>Just Right</i>, "Laugh Laugh Laugh", <i>Mad</i>, <i>Mad Winter Edition</i></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-action="edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fkpop.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGOT7%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D4&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb show-info-icon" style="width: 220px" typeof="mw:File/Thumb"> <a class="mw-file-description image" href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/kpop/images/8/8b/GOT7_Just_Right_group_concept_photo_5.png/revision/latest?cb=20250309075309"><img alt="GOT7 Just Right group concept photo 5" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-key="GOT7_Just_Right_group_concept_photo_5.png" data-image-name="GOT7 Just Right group concept photo 5.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/kpop/images/8/8b/GOT7_Just_Right_group_concept_photo_5.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20250309075309" decoding="async" height="147" loading="lazy" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="220"/></a> <noscript><a class="mw-file-description image" href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/kpop/images/8/8b/GOT7_Just_Right_group_concept_photo_5.png/revision/latest?cb=20250309075309"><img alt="GOT7 Just Right group concept photo 5" class="thumbimage" data-image-key="GOT7_Just_Right_group_concept_photo_5.png" data-image-name="GOT7 Just Right group concept photo 5.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/kpop/images/8/8b/GOT7_Just_Right_group_concept_photo_5.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20250309075309" decoding="async" height="147" loading="lazy" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/kpop/images/8/8b/GOT7_Just_Right_group_concept_photo_5.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20250309075309" width="220"/></a></noscript> <figcaption class="thumbcaption"> <a class="info-icon" href="/wiki/File:GOT7_Just_Right_group_concept_photo_5.png"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> <p class="caption">Concept photo for <i><a href="/wiki/Just_Right" title="Just Right">Just Right</a></i></p> </figcaption> </figure>
<p>In January 2015, GOT7 had their first fanmeeting for the anniversary of their debut. The event, called "365+", was held at Olympic Park in Seoul.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-12"><a href="#cite_note-12"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>11<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> Shortly after, they held an Asia Showcase Tour with stops in Taipei, Shanghai and Hong Kong.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-13"><a href="#cite_note-13"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>12<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p><p>They released their second Japanese single "<a href="/wiki/Love_Train" title="Love Train">Love Train</a>" on June 10 and came back a month later with mini album <i><a href="/wiki/Just_Right" title="Just Right">Just Right</a></i>. The title track of the same name has lyrics that are "an ode to their female fans that assures them their looks and weight are perfect whatever they are".<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-14"><a href="#cite_note-14"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>13<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb mw-halign-left show-info-icon" style="width: 220px" typeof="mw:File/Thumb"> <a class="mw-file-description image" href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/kpop/images/d/de/GOT7_Mad_group_concept_photo_2.png/revision/latest?cb=20151205182627"><img alt="GOT7 Mad group concept photo 2" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-key="GOT7_Mad_group_concept_photo_2.png" data-image-name="GOT7 Mad group concept photo 2.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/kpop/images/d/de/GOT7_Mad_group_concept_photo_2.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20151205182627" decoding="async" height="147" loading="lazy" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="220"/></a> <noscript><a class="mw-file-description image" href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/kpop/images/d/de/GOT7_Mad_group_concept_photo_2.png/revision/latest?cb=20151205182627"><img alt="GOT7 Mad group concept photo 2" class="thumbimage" data-image-key="GOT7_Mad_group_concept_photo_2.png" data-image-name="GOT7 Mad group concept photo 2.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/kpop/images/d/de/GOT7_Mad_group_concept_photo_2.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20151205182627" decoding="async" height="147" loading="lazy" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/kpop/images/d/de/GOT7_Mad_group_concept_photo_2.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20151205182627" width="220"/></a></noscript> <figcaption class="thumbcaption"> <a class="info-icon" href="/wiki/File:GOT7_Mad_group_concept_photo_2.png"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> <p class="caption">Concept photo for <i><a href="/wiki/Mad" title="Mad">Mad</a></i></p> </figcaption> </figure><p>They attended KCON in Los Angeles in the summer.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-15"><a href="#cite_note-15"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>14<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p><p>GOT7 released a third Japanese single titled "<a href="/wiki/Laugh_Laugh_Laugh" title="Laugh Laugh Laugh">Laugh Laugh Laugh</a>" on September 23 before releasing, on September 29, the mini album <i><a href="/wiki/Mad" title="Mad">Mad</a></i>. It was their second album to hit number 1 on the Billboard World Albums Chart<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-16"><a href="#cite_note-16"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>15<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> and they got their first ever music show win with its title track, "If You Do".<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-17"><a href="#cite_note-17"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>16<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> The album’s repackage, <i><a href="/wiki/Mad_Winter_Edition" title="Mad Winter Edition">Mad Winter Edition</a></i>, was released on November 23 and featured three new tracks along with a remastered version of "If You Do".
</p>
<h3><span id="2016:_Moriagatteyo.2C_Flight_Log:_Departure.2C_1st_World_Tour.2C_Flight_Log:_Turbulence.2C_Hey_Yah"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2016:_Moriagatteyo,_Flight_Log:_Departure,_1st_World_Tour,_Flight_Log:_Turbulence,_Hey_Yah">2016: <i>Moriagatteyo</i>, <i>Flight Log: Departure</i>, 1st World Tour, <i>Flight Log: Turbulence</i>, <i>Hey Yah</i></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-action="edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fkpop.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGOT7%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D5&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The group released their first full-length Japanese album <i><a href="/wiki/Moriagatteyo" title="Moriagatteyo">Moriagatteyo</a></i> on February 3. The tracklist featured songs from their previously released singles, Japanese versions of previous Korean title tracks as well as new tracks.
</p>
<figure class="thumb show-info-icon" style="width: 220px" typeof="mw:File/Thumb"> <a class="mw-file-description image" href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/kpop/images/2/2c/GOT7_Flight_Log_Arrival_group_concept_photo_1.png/revision/latest?cb=20210425200321"><img alt="GOT7 Flight Log Arrival group concept photo 1" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-key="GOT7_Flight_Log_Arrival_group_concept_photo_1.png" data-image-name="GOT7 Flight Log Arrival group concept photo 1.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/kpop/images/2/2c/GOT7_Flight_Log_Arrival_group_concept_photo_1.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20210425200321" decoding="async" height="147" loading="lazy" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="220"/></a> <noscript><a class="mw-file-description image" href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/kpop/images/2/2c/GOT7_Flight_Log_Arrival_group_concept_photo_1.png/revision/latest?cb=20210425200321"><img alt="GOT7 Flight Log Arrival group concept photo 1" class="thumbimage" data-image-key="GOT7_Flight_Log_Arrival_group_concept_photo_1.png" data-image-name="GOT7 Flight Log Arrival group concept photo 1.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/kpop/images/2/2c/GOT7_Flight_Log_Arrival_group_concept_photo_1.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20210425200321" decoding="async" height="147" loading="lazy" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/kpop/images/2/2c/GOT7_Flight_Log_Arrival_group_concept_photo_1.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20210425200321" width="220"/></a></noscript> <figcaption class="thumbcaption"> <a class="info-icon" href="/wiki/File:GOT7_Flight_Log_Arrival_group_concept_photo_1.png"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> <p class="caption">Concept photo for <i><a href="/wiki/Flight_Log:_Departure" title="Flight Log: Departure">Flight Log: Departure</a></i></p> </figcaption> </figure>
<p>They announced their next album, <i><a href="/wiki/Flight_Log:_Departure" title="Flight Log: Departure">Flight Log: Departure</a></i>, at the end of February, and it was released on March 21.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-18"><a href="#cite_note-18"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>17<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> For the first time, the members contributed to writing and composing many of the tracks.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-19"><a href="#cite_note-19"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>18<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> "Fly", the title track, earned nine music show wins.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-:0_20-0"><a href="#cite_note-:0-20"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>19<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> The group revealed their official light stick, in the shape of a transparent bird with a green light inside,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-21"><a href="#cite_note-21"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>20<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> and then, a few days later, they kicked off their first world tour on April 28, in Seoul. Leader JB suffered a spinal disk injury and, additionally to being pulled out of the last music shows performances, he could not participate in the first few concerts, that were held in Seoul. A full refund was offered to fans should they wish not to attend the concert because of JB’s absence, but reports showed an attendance of ten thousand people. As it was rated as an attendance rate of 100 percent, it is possible that no one refunded their tickets.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-:0_20-1"><a href="#cite_note-:0-20"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>19<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-22"><a href="#cite_note-22"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>21<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> Shows were sold out around the world.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-23"><a href="#cite_note-23"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>22<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p><p>GOT7 came back on September 27 with <i><a href="/wiki/Flight_Log:_Turbulence" title="Flight Log: Turbulence">Flight Log: Turbulence</a></i>, the second part of the trilogy started with <i><a href="/wiki/Flight_Log:_Departure" title="Flight Log: Departure">Flight Log: Departure</a></i>. They continued developing their potential as songwriters and composers as they participated in the creation of all but two of the tracks on the album.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-24"><a href="#cite_note-24"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>23<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p><p>Their first Japanese mini album, <i><a href="/wiki/Hey_Yah" title="Hey Yah">Hey Yah</a></i>, was released on November 16.
</p>
<h3><span id="2017:_Flight_Log:_Arrival.2C_.22My_Swagger.22.2C_7_for_7.2C_Jackson.27s_hiatus.2C_Turn_Up"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2017:_Flight_Log:_Arrival,_&quot;My_Swagger&quot;,_7_for_7,_Jackson's_hiatus,_Turn_Up">2017: <i>Flight Log: Arrival</i>, "My Swagger", <i>7 for 7</i>, Jackson's hiatus, <i>Turn Up</i></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-action="edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fkpop.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGOT7%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D6&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The 'Flight Log' trilogy was completed on March 13, 2017, with the release of mini album <i><a href="/wiki/Flight_Log:_Arrival" title="Flight Log: Arrival">Flight Log: Arrival</a></i>.
</p><p>"<a href="/wiki/My_Swagger" title="My Swagger">My Swagger</a>", their fourth Japanese single, was released on May 24.
</p><p>The sub-unit <a href="/wiki/JJ_Project" title="JJ Project">JJ Project</a> made a comeback on July 31 with mini album <i><a href="/wiki/Verse_2" title="Verse 2">Verse 2</a></i>.
</p><p>Jackson made his solo debut on August 26 with the single "<a href="/wiki/Papillon_(Jackson_Wang)" title="Papillon (Jackson Wang)">Papillon</a>".
</p>
<figure class="thumb mw-halign-left show-info-icon" style="width: 220px" typeof="mw:File/Thumb"> <a class="mw-file-description image" href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/kpop/images/e/ef/GOT7_7_for_7_group_concept_photo_1.png/revision/latest?cb=20200526121303"><img alt="GOT7 7 for 7 group concept photo 1" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-key="GOT7_7_for_7_group_concept_photo_1.png" data-image-name="GOT7 7 for 7 group concept photo 1.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/kpop/images/e/ef/GOT7_7_for_7_group_concept_photo_1.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20200526121303" decoding="async" height="147" loading="lazy" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="220"/></a> <noscript><a class="mw-file-description image" href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/kpop/images/e/ef/GOT7_7_for_7_group_concept_photo_1.png/revision/latest?cb=20200526121303"><img alt="GOT7 7 for 7 group concept photo 1" class="thumbimage" data-image-key="GOT7_7_for_7_group_concept_photo_1.png" data-image-name="GOT7 7 for 7 group concept photo 1.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/kpop/images/e/ef/GOT7_7_for_7_group_concept_photo_1.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20200526121303" decoding="async" height="147" loading="lazy" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/kpop/images/e/ef/GOT7_7_for_7_group_concept_photo_1.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20200526121303" width="220"/></a></noscript> <figcaption class="thumbcaption"> <a class="info-icon" href="/wiki/File:GOT7_7_for_7_group_concept_photo_1.png"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> <p class="caption">Concept photo for <i><a href="/wiki/7_for_7" title="7 for 7">7 for 7</a></i></p> </figcaption> </figure>
<p>On October 10, <i><a href="/wiki/7_for_7" title="7 for 7">7 for 7</a></i> was released. The title track was called "You Are" and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/JB" title="JB">JB</a> participated in its songwriting and composition. He explained that the lyrics are about someone that becomes the reason for one’s existence, and can be interpreted in multiple ways: it could be GOT7 and their fans, about family, or about two people in a relationship.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-25"><a href="#cite_note-25"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>24<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> <a href="/wiki/BamBam" title="BamBam">BamBam</a> also produced a lyric video for the track.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-26"><a href="#cite_note-26"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>25<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p><p>Because he founded his own label, Team Wang, and started promoting solo, Jackson had an extremely busy schedule.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-27"><a href="#cite_note-27"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>26<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> In order to "maintain his health condition",<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-:2_28-0"><a href="#cite_note-:2-28"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>27<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> he decided to withdraw from all future Japanese promotions. GOT7's second Japanese mini album, <i><a href="/wiki/Turn_Up" title="Turn Up">Turn Up</a></i>, was released on November 15 and it was the first Japanese release Jackson was not a part of.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-:2_28-1"><a href="#cite_note-:2-28"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>27<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="2018:_.22One_And_Only_You.22.2C_Eyes_On_You.2C_2nd_World_Tour.2C_Present_:_You.2C_Present_:_You_.26_Me_Edition"></span><span class="mw-headline" id='2018:_"One_And_Only_You",_Eyes_On_You,_2nd_World_Tour,_Present_:_You,_Present_:_You_&amp;_Me_Edition'>2018: "One And Only You", <i>Eyes On You</i>, 2nd World Tour, <i>Present : You</i>, <i>Present : You &amp; Me Edition</i></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-action="edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fkpop.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGOT7%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D7&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb show-info-icon" style="width: 175px" typeof="mw:File/Thumb"> <a class="mw-file-description image" href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/kpop/images/2/27/GOT7_Eyes_On_Me_group_concept_photo.png/revision/latest?cb=20180312173817"><img alt="GOT7 Eyes On Me group concept photo" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-key="GOT7_Eyes_On_Me_group_concept_photo.png" data-image-name="GOT7 Eyes On Me group concept photo.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/kpop/images/2/27/GOT7_Eyes_On_Me_group_concept_photo.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/175?cb=20180312173817" decoding="async" height="220" loading="lazy" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="175"/></a> <noscript><a class="mw-file-description image" href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/kpop/images/2/27/GOT7_Eyes_On_Me_group_concept_photo.png/revision/latest?cb=20180312173817"><img alt="GOT7 Eyes On Me group concept photo" class="thumbimage" data-image-key="GOT7_Eyes_On_Me_group_concept_photo.png" data-image-name="GOT7 Eyes On Me group concept photo.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/kpop/images/2/27/GOT7_Eyes_On_Me_group_concept_photo.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/175?cb=20180312173817" decoding="async" height="220" loading="lazy" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/kpop/images/2/27/GOT7_Eyes_On_Me_group_concept_photo.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/175?cb=20180312173817" width="175"/></a></noscript> <figcaption class="thumbcaption"> <a class="info-icon" href="/wiki/File:GOT7_Eyes_On_Me_group_concept_photo.png"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> <p class="caption">Concept photo for <i><a href="/wiki/Eyes_On_You_(GOT7)" title="Eyes On You (GOT7)">Eyes On You</a></i></p> </figcaption> </figure>
<p>"<a href="/wiki/One_And_Only_You" title="One And Only You">One And Only You</a>", a pre-release track featuring <a href="/wiki/Hyolyn" title="Hyolyn">Hyolyn</a> for their upcoming album <i><a href="/wiki/Eyes_On_You_(GOT7)" title="Eyes On You (GOT7)">Eyes On You</a></i>, was released on February 28. The album was released on March 12 with the title track "Look". Their second world tour was kicked off on May 4, in Seoul. Their last stop was on August 24, in Hong Kong.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-29"><a href="#cite_note-29"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>28<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> With concerts held in between dates of their world tour, they also had a Japanese tour, during which they released the single "<a href="/wiki/The_New_Era" title="The New Era">The New Era</a>".<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-30"><a href="#cite_note-30"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>29<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb mw-halign-left show-info-icon" style="width: 220px" typeof="mw:File/Thumb"> <a class="mw-file-description image" href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/kpop/images/5/54/GOT7_Present_You_group_concept_photo_2.png/revision/latest?cb=20180917175318"><img alt="GOT7 Present You group concept photo 2" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-key="GOT7_Present_You_group_concept_photo_2.png" data-image-name="GOT7 Present You group concept photo 2.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/kpop/images/5/54/GOT7_Present_You_group_concept_photo_2.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20180917175318" decoding="async" height="147" loading="lazy" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="220"/></a> <noscript><a class="mw-file-description image" href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/kpop/images/5/54/GOT7_Present_You_group_concept_photo_2.png/revision/latest?cb=20180917175318"><img alt="GOT7 Present You group concept photo 2" class="thumbimage" data-image-key="GOT7_Present_You_group_concept_photo_2.png" data-image-name="GOT7 Present You group concept photo 2.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/kpop/images/5/54/GOT7_Present_You_group_concept_photo_2.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20180917175318" decoding="async" height="147" loading="lazy" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/kpop/images/5/54/GOT7_Present_You_group_concept_photo_2.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20180917175318" width="220"/></a></noscript> <figcaption class="thumbcaption"> <a class="info-icon" href="/wiki/File:GOT7_Present_You_group_concept_photo_2.png"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> <p class="caption">Concept photo for <i><a href="/wiki/Present_:_You" title="Present : You">Present : You</a></i></p> </figcaption> </figure>
<p><i><a href="/wiki/Present_:_You" title="Present : You">Present : You</a></i>, their second full-length album, was released on September 17. The album features versions of its title track in four different languages, Korean, English, Mandarin and Spanish. It also features a solo song by each of the members. Each member participated to the creation of his own track. Additionally to the music video of the title track, "Lullaby", seven other music videos were released, one for each of the solo tracks.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-31"><a href="#cite_note-31"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>30<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p><p><i>Present: You</i>’s repackage, <i><a href="/wiki/Present_:_You_%26_Me_Edition" title="Present : You &amp; Me Edition">Present : You &amp; Me Edition</a></i>, was released on December 3.
</p>
<h3><span id="2019:_I_Won.27t_Let_You_Go.2C_Spinning_Top_:_Between_Security_.26_Insecurity.2C_3rd_world_tour.2C_Love_Loop.2C_Call_My_Name.2C_.22Sing_for_U.22.2C_Love_Loop_.7ESing_for_U_Special_Edition.7E"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2019:_I_Won't_Let_You_Go,_Spinning_Top_:_Between_Security_&amp;_Insecurity,_3rd_world_tour,_Love_Loop,_Call_My_Name,_&quot;Sing_for_U&quot;,_Love_Loop_~Sing_for_U_Special_Edition~">2019: <i>I Won't Let You Go</i>, <i>Spinning Top : Between Security &amp; Insecurity</i>, 3rd world tour, <i>Love Loop</i>, <i>Call My Name</i>, "Sing for U", <i>Love Loop ~Sing for U Special Edition~</i></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-action="edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fkpop.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGOT7%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D8&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>GOT7’s third Japanese mini album, <i><a href="/wiki/I_Won%27t_Let_You_Go" title="I Won't Let You Go">I Won't Let You Go</a></i>, was released on January 30.
</p><p>On March 5, the group’s second sub-unit, <a href="/wiki/Jus2" title="Jus2">Jus2</a>, debuted with mini album <a href="/wiki/Focus_(Jus2)" title="Focus (Jus2)"><i>Focus</i></a>.
</p>
<figure class="thumb show-info-icon" style="width: 220px" typeof="mw:File/Thumb"> <a class="mw-file-description image" href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/kpop/images/7/71/GOT7_Spinning_Top_Between_Security_%26_Insecurity_group_concept_photo_1.png/revision/latest?cb=20200526110451"><img alt="GOT7 Spinning Top Between Security &amp; Insecurity group concept photo 1" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-key="GOT7_Spinning_Top_Between_Security_%26_Insecurity_group_concept_photo_1.png" data-image-name="GOT7 Spinning Top Between Security &amp; Insecurity group concept photo 1.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/kpop/images/7/71/GOT7_Spinning_Top_Between_Security_%26_Insecurity_group_concept_photo_1.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20200526110451" decoding="async" height="147" loading="lazy" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="220"/></a> <noscript><a class="mw-file-description image" href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/kpop/images/7/71/GOT7_Spinning_Top_Between_Security_%26_Insecurity_group_concept_photo_1.png/revision/latest?cb=20200526110451"><img alt="GOT7 Spinning Top Between Security &amp; Insecurity group concept photo 1" class="thumbimage" data-image-key="GOT7_Spinning_Top_Between_Security_%26_Insecurity_group_concept_photo_1.png" data-image-name="GOT7 Spinning Top Between Security &amp; Insecurity group concept photo 1.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/kpop/images/7/71/GOT7_Spinning_Top_Between_Security_%26_Insecurity_group_concept_photo_1.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20200526110451" decoding="async" height="147" loading="lazy" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/kpop/images/7/71/GOT7_Spinning_Top_Between_Security_%26_Insecurity_group_concept_photo_1.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20200526110451" width="220"/></a></noscript> <figcaption class="thumbcaption"> <a class="info-icon" href="/wiki/File:GOT7_Spinning_Top_Between_Security_%26_Insecurity_group_concept_photo_1.png"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> <p class="caption">Concept photo for <i><a href="/wiki/Spinning_Top_:_Between_Security_%26_Insecurity" title="Spinning Top : Between Security &amp; Insecurity">Spinning Top : Between Security &amp; Insecurity</a></i></p> </figcaption> </figure>
<p><i><a href="/wiki/Spinning_Top_:_Between_Security_%26_Insecurity" title="Spinning Top : Between Security &amp; Insecurity">Spinning Top : Between Security &amp; Insecurity</a></i> was released on May 20 and was followed by GOT7’s third world tour, called "Keep Spinning", starting on June 15, in Seoul.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-32"><a href="#cite_note-32"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>31<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> Like during their previous world tour, they kicked off a Japanese tour in between the "Keep Spinning" world tour, releasing the Japanese mini album <i><a href="/wiki/Love_Loop" title="Love Loop">Love Loop</a></i> on July 31.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-33"><a href="#cite_note-33"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>32<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> Because of safety concerns, world tour concerts in Hong Kong, originally scheduled on August 31 and September 1, were postponed.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-34"><a href="#cite_note-34"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>33<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p><p>They released mini album <i><a href="/wiki/Call_My_Name_(GOT7)" title="Call My Name (GOT7)">Call My Name</a></i> on November 4. Described by Yugyeom as a sorrowful and sexy concept, its title track has a sound more simple and minimal than usual, according to JB.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-35"><a href="#cite_note-35"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>34<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p><p><i><a href="/wiki/Love_Loop_~Sing_for_U_Special_Edition~" title="Love Loop ~Sing for U Special Edition~">Love Loop ~Sing for U Special Edition~</a></i>, a repackage of <i>Love Loop</i>, was released on December 18, with the track "<a href="/wiki/Sing_for_U" title="Sing for U">Sing for U</a>" having been released on October 21 as a pre-release track.
</p>
<h3><span id="2020:_Dye.2C_Breath_of_Love_:_Last_Piece"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2020:_Dye,_Breath_of_Love_:_Last_Piece">2020: <i>Dye</i>, <i>Breath of Love : Last Piece</i></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-action="edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fkpop.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGOT7%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D9&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Mark made his solo debut on January 11 with the digital single "<a href="/wiki/Outta_My_Head" title="Outta My Head">Outta My Head</a>".
</p>
<figure class="thumb mw-halign-left show-info-icon" style="width: 220px" typeof="mw:File/Thumb"> <a class="mw-file-description image" href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/kpop/images/9/9d/GOT7_Dye_promotional_photo.png/revision/latest?cb=20200526111539"><img alt="GOT7 Dye promotional photo" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-key="GOT7_Dye_promotional_photo.png" data-image-name="GOT7 Dye promotional photo.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/kpop/images/9/9d/GOT7_Dye_promotional_photo.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20200526111539" decoding="async" height="150" loading="lazy" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="220"/></a> <noscript><a class="mw-file-description image" href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/kpop/images/9/9d/GOT7_Dye_promotional_photo.png/revision/latest?cb=20200526111539"><img alt="GOT7 Dye promotional photo" class="thumbimage" data-image-key="GOT7_Dye_promotional_photo.png" data-image-name="GOT7 Dye promotional photo.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/kpop/images/9/9d/GOT7_Dye_promotional_photo.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20200526111539" decoding="async" height="150" loading="lazy" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/kpop/images/9/9d/GOT7_Dye_promotional_photo.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20200526111539" width="220"/></a></noscript> <figcaption class="thumbcaption"> <a class="info-icon" href="/wiki/File:GOT7_Dye_promotional_photo.png"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> <p class="caption">Concept photo for <i><a href="/wiki/Dye" title="Dye">Dye</a></i></p> </figcaption> </figure>
<p>Amid coronavirus concerns, remaining concerts of the "Keep Spinning" world tour were postponed.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-36"><a href="#cite_note-36"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>35<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p><p>A cinema trailer for GOT7’s eleventh mini album was released on April 5,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-37"><a href="#cite_note-37"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>36<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> followed by teasers in the form of cinema scripts, regular individual and unit teaser photos and lyrics teasers. The narration in the cinema trailer and the quotes in the cinema scripts come from Shakespeare’s <i>Romeo and Juliet</i><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-38"><a href="#cite_note-38"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>37<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> and the album has a "medieval ballad concept".<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-:1_39-0"><a href="#cite_note-:1-39"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>38<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> "Including the lead single, the album's 10 tracks come as a sequence of love stories as if reading a classical romance novel, according to Yugyeom."<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-:1_39-1"><a href="#cite_note-:1-39"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>38<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> Four of the ten tracks are exclusive to the CD version<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-40"><a href="#cite_note-40"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>39<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> and are solo or sub-unit songs that were already showcased during the world tour.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-:1_39-2"><a href="#cite_note-:1-39"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>38<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p><p>The release of the album <i><a href="/wiki/Breath_of_Love_:_Last_Piece" title="Breath of Love : Last Piece">Breath of Love : Last Piece</a></i> and its pre-release, "<a href="/wiki/Breath_(GOT7)" title="Breath (GOT7)">Breath</a>", was first announced on November 8. "Breath" was released on November 23, and the album on November 30.
</p>
<h3><span id="2021:_Departure_from_JYP_Entertainment.2C_.22Encore.22"></span><span class="mw-headline" id='2021:_Departure_from_JYP_Entertainment,_"Encore"'>2021: Departure from JYP Entertainment, "Encore"</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-action="edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fkpop.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGOT7%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D10&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb show-info-icon" style="width: 220px" typeof="mw:File/Thumb"> <a class="mw-file-description image" href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/kpop/images/e/ed/GOT7_Encore_promotional_photo.png/revision/latest?cb=20210220024234"><img alt="GOT7 Encore promotional photo" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-key="GOT7_Encore_promotional_photo.png" data-image-name="GOT7 Encore promotional photo.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/kpop/images/e/ed/GOT7_Encore_promotional_photo.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20210220024234" decoding="async" height="220" loading="lazy" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="220"/></a> <noscript><a class="mw-file-description image" href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/kpop/images/e/ed/GOT7_Encore_promotional_photo.png/revision/latest?cb=20210220024234"><img alt="GOT7 Encore promotional photo" class="thumbimage" data-image-key="GOT7_Encore_promotional_photo.png" data-image-name="GOT7 Encore promotional photo.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/kpop/images/e/ed/GOT7_Encore_promotional_photo.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20210220024234" decoding="async" height="220" loading="lazy" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/kpop/images/e/ed/GOT7_Encore_promotional_photo.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20210220024234" width="220"/></a></noscript> <figcaption class="thumbcaption"> <a class="info-icon" href="/wiki/File:GOT7_Encore_promotional_photo.png"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> <p class="caption">Concept photo for "<a href="/wiki/Encore_(GOT7)" title="Encore (GOT7)">Encore</a>"</p> </figcaption> </figure>
<p>On January 10, it was reported by <i>Dispatch</i> that all members of the group would be leaving <a href="/wiki/JYP_Entertainment" title="JYP Entertainment">JYP Entertainment</a> after 7 years of contract, with the 35th Golden Disc Awards being their last activity as a group.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-41"><a href="#cite_note-41"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>40<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> On January 11, JYP Entertainment officially announced that the members will be leaving the agency as their contract expires on January 19.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-42"><a href="#cite_note-42"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>41<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p><p>On February 20 at midnight KST, the MV teaser for "<a href="/wiki/Encore_(GOT7)" title="Encore (GOT7)">Encore</a>" was released on the group's new YouTube channel. The single, which was released at 6PM KST on the same day, was their first release since leaving JYP Entertainment.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-43"><a href="#cite_note-43"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>42<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> The song is about their love for their fans and their desire to keep singing for them.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-44"><a href="#cite_note-44"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>43<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> It was also their first release since the leader JB changed his stage name to JAY B.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-45"><a href="#cite_note-45"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>44<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="2022:_GOT7">2022: <i>GOT7</i></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-action="edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fkpop.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGOT7%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D11&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb mw-halign-left show-info-icon" style="width: 220px" typeof="mw:File/Thumb"> <a class="mw-file-description image" href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/kpop/images/7/7c/GOT7_GOT7_group_concept_photo_1.png/revision/latest?cb=20220514151611"><img alt="GOT7 GOT7 group concept photo 1" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-key="GOT7_GOT7_group_concept_photo_1.png" data-image-name="GOT7 GOT7 group concept photo 1.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/kpop/images/7/7c/GOT7_GOT7_group_concept_photo_1.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20220514151611" decoding="async" height="147" loading="lazy" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="220"/></a> <noscript><a class="mw-file-description image" href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/kpop/images/7/7c/GOT7_GOT7_group_concept_photo_1.png/revision/latest?cb=20220514151611"><img alt="GOT7 GOT7 group concept photo 1" class="thumbimage" data-image-key="GOT7_GOT7_group_concept_photo_1.png" data-image-name="GOT7 GOT7 group concept photo 1.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/kpop/images/7/7c/GOT7_GOT7_group_concept_photo_1.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20220514151611" decoding="async" height="147" loading="lazy" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/kpop/images/7/7c/GOT7_GOT7_group_concept_photo_1.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20220514151611" width="220"/></a></noscript> <figcaption class="thumbcaption"> <a class="info-icon" href="/wiki/File:GOT7_GOT7_group_concept_photo_1.png"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> <p class="caption">Concept photo for <i><a href="/wiki/GOT7_(EP)" title="GOT7 (EP)">GOT7</a></i></p> </figcaption> </figure>
<p>On April 22, JoyNews24 reported that GOT7 would be making a full-group comeback this May and were in the final stage of preparations, with music production being almost done.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-46"><a href="#cite_note-46"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>45<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>  On May 6, they opened new SNS accounts, and it was revealed that GOT7 had signed with <a href="/wiki/Warner_Music_Korea" title="Warner Music Korea">Warner Music Korea</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-47"><a href="#cite_note-47"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>46<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>  Three days later, a teaser was revealed for their new self-titled EP, <i><a href="/wiki/GOT7_(EP)" title="GOT7 (EP)">GOT7</a></i>, set to be released on May 23.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-48"><a href="#cite_note-48"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>47<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> The album, of which all the songs were created by the members, reflects the identity and color of GOT7 as a group, which is why that title was chosen.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-49"><a href="#cite_note-49"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>48<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p><p>On May 10, they announced their Seoul's fancon, Homecoming with I GOT 7, happening on May 21 and 22.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-50"><a href="#cite_note-50"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>49<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="2023:_Enlistments.2C_new_light_stick"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2023:_Enlistments,_new_light_stick">2023: Enlistments, new light stick</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-action="edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fkpop.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGOT7%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D12&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In the beginning of February, <a href="/wiki/JAY_B" title="JAY B">JAY B</a> started his military service, becoming the first member of the group to do so.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-51"><a href="#cite_note-51"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>50<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Jinyoung_(GOT7)" title="Jinyoung (GOT7)">Jinyoung</a> enlisted three months later, on May 8.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-52"><a href="#cite_note-52"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>51<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p><p>On September 4, the group announced the new version of their light stick through their social media.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-53"><a href="#cite_note-53"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>52<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="2025:_Winter_Heptagon">2025: <i>Winter Heptagon</i></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-action="edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fkpop.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGOT7%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D13&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>On November 7, 2024, as member <a href="/wiki/Jinyoung_(GOT7)" title="Jinyoung (GOT7)">Jinyoung</a> as discharged from the military, he revealed that GOT7 is currently preparing to have a comeback in 2025, before the remaining members start their military service.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-54"><a href="#cite_note-54"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>53<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> On December 7, members JAY B and BamBam confirmed that the group will be returning on January 20.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-55"><a href="#cite_note-55"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>54<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> They started teasing their return on December 19.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-56"><a href="#cite_note-56"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>55<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> On December 20, GOT7 announced that they will be releasing their 12th mini album <i><a href="/wiki/Winter_Heptagon" title="Winter Heptagon">Winter Heptagon</a></i>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-57"><a href="#cite_note-57"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>56<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="EPs">EPs</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-action="edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fkpop.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGOT7%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D20&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
